            <change when="2020-11-04" who="Dominik Wujastyk">Began this file.</change>
            <change when="2023-11-04" who="Dominik Wujastyk"> added 1.41, based on MS
                N</change>
            <change when="2023-06-26" who="Dominik Wujastyk">Separated the file into two
                parts, 1-31 and 32-end, because of processing limits at Saktumiva</change>
            <change when="2023-10-25" who="Dominik Wujastyk">Added all remaining adhyāyas
                from H and stripped out transcription codes to make draft provisional
                edition files.</change>
            <change when="2024-03-27" who="Dominik Wujastyk">Completed a major overhaul
                ("meta-edit") of the all Sūtrasthāna files. I checked all passages and
                made sure that xml:id tags matched correctly across all files, unifying
                and separating text-portions as needed. I separated words ad hoc. I
                corrected readings and checked against the MSS in many cases, but again ad
                hoc. There is much remaining to be done, but the Sūtrasthāna is now in a
                coherent format at the macro scale.</change>

        <body>
            <div n="1" type="sthāna">
                <head xml:lang="en">[Sūtrasthāna 32-end]</head>
                <div n="32" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 32, draft based on MS H]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.32.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athātaḥ svabhāvavipratipattiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.3-4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.32.3-4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         svabhāvaprasiddhānāṃ śarīraikadeśānām anyathātvaṃ maraṇāya | tad
                        yathā śuklānāṃ kṛṣṇatvaṃ kṛṣṇānāṃ śuklatvaṃ | sthirāṇām mṛdutvaṃ |
                        calānām acalatvam acalānāñ calatvaṃ | pṛthūnāṃ saṃkṣiptatvaṃ
                        saṃkṣiptānāṃ pṛthutvaṃ | dīrghāṇāṃ hrasvatvaṃ ca hrasvānāṃ
                        dīrghatā | apatanadharmmiṇāṃ patanam akasmāc
                        chaityoṣṇasneharaukṣyaprastambhavaivarṇṇyāni apasarppaṇam aṅgānāṃ
                        svebhyaḥ sthānebhyaḥ śarīraikadeśānām
                        avasraṃsotkṣiptabhrāntapatitavimuktanirggamātigamagurulaghutvāni
                        pravālavarṇṇavyaṅgaprādurbbhāvo vākasmāt sirāṇāṃ ca darśana lalāṭe
                        nāsāvaṃśe vā piṭakotpattir udakotpattir nnetrarogam
                        vināsrupravṛttir lalāṭe vā prabhātakāle svedapravṛttiḥ |
                        gomayacūrṇṇaprakāśasya rajaso darśanam uttamāṅge līyanam vā
                        kapotakaṅkagṛddhraprabhṛtīnāṃ mūtrapurīṣapravṛddhir abhuñjanānāṃ
                        stanamūlahṛdayorassu ca śūlotpattayaḥ | madhye śūnatvam anteṣu
                        parimlāyitvaṃ | viparyayo vā naṣṭahīnavikalavihṛtasvaraṃ vā
                        vivarṇṇapuṣpaprādurbbhāvo vā dantanakhaśarīreṣu puṣpadarśanaṃ
                        yasya cāpsu kaphaśakṛdretāṃsi nimajjanti yasya ca dṛṣṭimaṇḍale
                        bhinnavikṛtāni rūpāṇy ālocyante snehābhyaktakeśāṅga iva yo bhāti
                        yaś ca durbbalo bhaktadveṣātisārābhyām pīḍyate | kāsamānaś ca
                        tṛṣṇātibhūtaḥ kṣīṇaś charddibhaktadeśayuktaḥ saphenarudhirodvāmī
                        hatasvaraḥ śūlābhihataś ca manuṣyaśūnakaracaraṇo nnadveṣī
                        srastapiṇḍakāṃsapāṇipādaḥ | yaś ca pūrvāhṇe bhuktam aparāhṇe
                        ścharddayaty avidagdhaṃ sāryate vā jvarakāsābhibhūtaḥ sa śvāsān
                        mriyate | vastavad vilapamāno bhūmau patati srastamuṣkaḥ
                        stabdhaśepo bhagnagrīvaḥ praṇaṣṭamehaś ca manuṣyaḥ
                        prāgviśuṣyamāṇahṛdaya ārddraśarīraḥ | yaś ca loṣṭaṃ
                        loṣṭenābhihanti | kāṣṭham vā kāṣṭhena tṛṇāni vā cchinnanti |
                        adharoṣṭham vā daśati uttaroṣṭham vā leḍhi | āluñcati karṇṇau
                        keśām̐ś ca | devadvijagurusuhṛdvaidyān vā vidveṣṭi yasya ca
                        vakrānuvakragā grahā garhitasthānagatāḥ | janmaṛkṣam
                        vāsyolkāśanibhyām abhihanyate | rātrau vā
                        gṛhadvāraśayanāsanayānavāhanamaṇiratnopakaraṇagarhitalakṣaṇanimittaprādurbbhāvo
                        veti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.32.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavanti cātra ||
                        <caesura/>
                         cikitsyamānaḥ samyak tu vikāro yo 'bhivarddhate |
                        <caesura/>
                         prakṣīṇabala<pc> </pc>māṃsasya lakṣaṇan tadgatāyuṣaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.32.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nivarttate mahāvyādhiḥ sahasā yasya dehinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         na cāhāraphalaṃ yasya dṛśyate sa vinaśyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.32.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         etāni riṣṭarūpāṇi samyag budhyeta yo bhiṣak |
                        <caesura/>
                         sādhyāsādhyaparīkṣañ ca sa rājñaḥ sammato bhaved iti || 31 || ❈
                        || </l>
                </div>
                <div n="33" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 33, draft based on MS H]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1.33.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto vāraṇīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.33.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         upadravais tu ye juṣṭā-vyādhayo yānty avāryatāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rasāyanair vvinā vatsa tāṃ śṛṇv ekamanā mama || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.33.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vātavyādhiḥ pramehaś ca kuṣṭhānyatha bhagandaraṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         arśośmarī mūḍhagarbho bhavaty udaram aṣṭamam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.33.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         aṣṭāv ete mahāntaḥ syūr vvyādhayo dustarāḥ sadā |
                        prāṇamāṃsakṣayaḥ śophas tṛṣṇā ccharddir jvaras tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.33.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atīsāraś ca mūrcchā ca hikkāśvāsas tathaiva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         etair upadravair jjuṣṭān sarvvān etān vivarjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.33.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śūnaṃ suptatvacam bhagnaṅ kampādhmānanipīḍitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rujārttam antañ ca naram vātavyādhir vvināśayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.33.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yathoktopadravāviṣṭam atiprasrutam eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         piṭakāpīḍitaṃ gāḍhaṃ prameho hanti mānavaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.33.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prabhinnaṃ prasrutāṅgañ ca raktanetraṃ hatasvaraṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pañcakarmmaguṇātītaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ hanti hi kuṣṭhinaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.33.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vātamūtrapurīṣāṇi krimayaḥ śukram eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhagandarāt prasravanti sa naśyati bhagandarī || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.33.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tṛṣṇarocakaśūlārttam atiprasrutaśoṇitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śophātīsārasaṃyuktaṃ durnāmā kṣapayen naraṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.12">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.33.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         praśūnanābhivṛṣaṇaṃ vaddhamūtrarujāturaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         aśmarī kṣapayaty āśu sikatāśarkkarānvitaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.14">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.33.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pārśvabhaṅgānnavidveṣaḥ śophātīsārapīḍitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         vivarjayed udariṇam virikto yo 'bhipūryate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.13">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.33.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yonīsamvaraṇaṃ saṅgaḥ kukṣo makkallasaṃjñitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         hanyuḥ striyaṃ mūḍhaga-rvbhe yathoktāś cāpy upadravāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.15">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.33.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         visaṃjñas tām yate yas tu śete nipati-to yathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śītārddito 'ntaruṣṇaś ca jvareṇa mriyate naraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.16">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.33.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yo hṛṣṭaromā raktākṣo hṛdi saṃghātaśūlavān |
                        <caesura/>
                         vaktreṇa cocchvasiti taṃ jvaro hanti mānavaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.17">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.33.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hikkāśvāsa samāyuktaṃ mūḍham vibhrāntalocanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         santatocchvāsinaṃ kṣīṇaṃ naraṃ kṣapayate jvaraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.18"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.19">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.33.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śvāsaśūlapipāsārtaṃ-kṣīṇañ jvaranipīḍitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         viśeṣeṇa naraṃ vṛddham atīsāro vināśayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.20">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.33.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śuklākṣamannadveṣṭāram ūrddhaśvāsanipīḍitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛcchreṇa bahu mehantaṃ yakṣmā hantīha mānavaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.21">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.33.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śvāsaśūlapipāsānnavidveṣo granthimūḍhatā |
                        <caesura/>
                         jāyate durvvalatvaṃ ca gulmino maraṇāya vai|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.22">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.33.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ādhmānaṃ vaddhaniṣyandaṃ ccharddihikkātṛṣānvitam |
                        <caesura/>
                         rujāśvāsasamāyuktaṃ vidradhir nnāśayet naraṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.23">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.33.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pāṇḍudantanakho yastu pāṇḍunetraś ca mānavaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pāṇḍusaṃghātadarśī ca pāṇḍurogī vinaśyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.24">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.33.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         lohitañ charddayed yas tu bahuśo lohitekṣaṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         lohito 'ṅgāradarśī ca mriyate raktapaittikaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.25">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.33.25</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         avāco pi savāco 'pi kṣīṇamānsavalo naraḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         jāgarūko kṣyāsandeham unmādena vinaśyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.26">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.33.26</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         apasmarantam bahuśaḥ prakṣīṇañ calitaṃ bhruvaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         netrābhyāñ ca vikurvvāṇam apasmāro vināśayet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.trailer"> 33 ||</l>
                </div>
                <div n="34" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 34, draft based on MS H]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1.34.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto yuktasenīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.1.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1.34.1.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dhanvantarim mahāprājñaṃ sarvvaśāstraviśāradaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         caraṇāv upasaṃgṛhya suśrutaḥ paripṛcchati ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.34.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yuktasenasya nṛpateḥ parānabhijighāṃsataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhiṣajā rakṣaṇaṃ kāryaṃ yathā tad brūhi me mune ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.3.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1.34.3.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā prābravīd bhiṣajām varaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.34.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vijigīṣuḥ sahāmātyair yātrāyuktaḥ prayatnataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rakṣitavyo viśeṣeṇa viṣādeva narādhipaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.34.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         panthānam udakañ chāyāṃ bhaktaṃ yavasamindhanaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         duṣayanty arayas tāni jānīyāc chodhanīya ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya liṅgaṃ cikitsāñ ca kalpasthāne pravakṣyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.34.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ekottaraṃ mṛtyuśatam atharvvāṇaḥ pracakṣate |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatraikaḥ kālasaṃyuktaḥ śeṣās tv āgantavaḥ smṛtāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.34.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣāgantunimittebhyo rasamantraviśāradau |
                        <caesura/>
                         rakṣatāṃ nṛpatin nityaṃ yatnād vaidyapurohitau ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.34.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         brahmāvedāṅgamaṣṭāṅgam āyurvvedam pracakṣate |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmāt purohitamate vartteta bhiṣag ātmavān ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.34.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         saṅkaraḥ sarvvavarṇṇānāṃ vināśo dharmmakarmmiṇāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         prajanām api kṛcchrāṇi bhavanti nṛpanāśataḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.34.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         puruṣāṇān nṛpānāñ ca kevalan tulyamūrttitā |
                        <caesura/>
                         ājñātyāgaḥ kṣamā dhairyam vikramaś cāpy amānuṣaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.34.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmād devam ivābhīkṣṇam vāṅmanaḥ karmabhiḥ śubhaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         cintayet nṛpatim vaidyaḥ śreyāṃsīcchan vicakṣaṇaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.12">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.34.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         skandhāvāre ca mahati rājaveśma samīpataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavet sannihito vaidyaḥ sarvvopakaraṇānvitaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.13">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.34.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrastham enan dhvajavad yaśaḥkhyātibhir ucchritaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         upasarppantyamohena viṣaśalyāmayārdditāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.14">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.34.14</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         svatantrakuśalo 'nyeṣu śāstrārtheṣv abahiḥ kṛtaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vaidyo dhvajam ivābhāti nṛpatadvidyapūjitaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.15">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.34.15</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vaidyo vyādhyupasṛṣṭaś ca bhaiṣajam paricārakaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ete pādāś cikitsāyāḥ karmmasādhanahetavaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.16">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.34.16</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         guṇavadbhis tribhiḥ pādaiś caturthyo guṇavān bhiṣak |
                        <caesura/>
                         vyādhim alpena kālena mahāntam api sādhayet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.17">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.34.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vaidyahīnās trayaḥ pādā guṇavanto 'pyapārthakāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         udgātṛhotṛbrahmāṇo yathādhvaryam vinādhvare ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.18">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.34.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vaidyas tu guṇavāneko yāpayed āturaṃ sadā |
                        <caesura/>
                         plavam paricaran dhīraḥ karṇṇadhāram ivāmbhasi ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.19">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.34.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatvopagataśāstrārtho dṛṣṭakarmmā svayaṅkṛtī |
                        <caesura/>
                         laghuhastaḥ śuciḥ sūraḥ sajjopaskarabheṣajaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.20">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.34.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pratyutpannamatir ddhīmān vyavasāyī viśāradaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         satyadharmmaparo yaś ca sabhiṣak pāda ucyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.21">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.34.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         āyuṣmān satvavān sādhyo dravyavān mitravān api |
                        <caesura/>
                         vaidyavākyakṛd āstiṣko vyādhitaḥ pāda ucyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.22">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.34.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         praśastadeśasaṃbhūtaṃ praśaste kāla uddhṛtaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yuktamātram manaskāntaṅ gandhavarṇṇarasānvitaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.23">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.34.23</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         doṣaghnamaglāninikaram avikārya viparyayaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         samīkṣya dattaṅ kāle ca bheṣajam pāda ucyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.24">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.34.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snigdho 'jugupsur bbalavānyukto vyādhitarakṣaṇe |
                        <caesura/>
                         vaidyavākyakṛdaśrāntaḥ pādaḥ paricaraḥ smṛtaḥ ||</l>
                    <p ana="trailer">layka ||</p>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.35.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāta āturopakramaṇīyam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.35.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         āturam upakramamāṇena vaidyenāyurādāv eva tāvat parīsatyāyuṣi
                        vyādhyṛtvagnivayodehasatvavalasātmyaprakṛtibheṣajadeśān parīkṣeta
                        | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.35.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra
                        mahāpāṇipādapṛṣṭhastanāgrasukhadarśanaskandhalalāṭadīrghāṅguliparvvocchvāsaprekṣaṇavāhum
                        vistīrṇṇabhrūs tanāntaroraskaṃ hṛsvajaṅghāmeḍhragrīvaṅ
                        gambhīrasatvasvaranāsimanuccair vaddhas tanm upacitamahāromaṃ
                        romasakarṇṇe pārśva mastakaṃ snātānuliptaṃ mūrddham ānūpūrvyo
                        paścāc ca viśuṣyamāṇahṛdayam puruṣañ jānīyād dīrghāyuḥ khalv ayam
                        iti | tam ekāntena upakramet | tatra tail laikṣaṇair viparītair
                        alpayum miśrair mmadhyam āyur iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.35.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavanti cātra ||
                        <caesura/>
                         gūḍhasandhisirāsnāyuḥ saṃhatāṅgaḥ sthirendriyaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         uttarottarasukṣetro yaḥ sa dīrghāyur ucyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.35.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         garbhāt prabhṛtyarogo yaḥ śanaiḥ samabhivarddhate |
                        <caesura/>
                         śarīrajñānavijñānaiḥ sa dīrghāyuḥ samāsataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.35.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         madhyamasyāyuṣo jñāna mata ūrdhvan nibodha me |
                        <caesura/>
                         adhastād akṣayor yasya rekhāḥ suvyaktam āyatāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.35.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dve vā tisro 'dhikā vāpi pādau karṇau ca māṃsalau |
                        <caesura/>
                         nāsāgram ūrdhvañ ca bhavet rekhāś ca pṛṣṭhataḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.35.9</label>

                         yasya syus tasya vijñeyam āyur bhavati saptatiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         jaghanyaś cāyuṣo jñāna mata ūrdhvan nibodha me || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.35.10</label>

                         hṛsvāni yasya parvvāṇi sumahac cāpi mehanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         avalīḍham uroyaś ca na ca syāt pṛṣṭham āyataṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.35.11</label>

                        <caesura/>
                         hasato jalpato vāpi dantamānsam pradṛśyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.12ab">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.35.12ab</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         atha punar āyuṣo vijñānārtham aṅgapratyaṅgapramāṇasāra
                        anupadekṣyāmaḥ || tatra aṅgātyantarādhiśakthivāhuśirāṃsi tad
                        avayavāḥ pratyaṅgāni svair aṅgulaiḥ pādāṅguṣṭhapradeśinyau
                        dvaṅgulāyate | pradeśinyās tu madhyamānāmikākaniṣṭhikā pūrvvataḥ |
                        pañcañ bhāgahīnācaturaṅgulāyate | pañcaṅgulavismṛte | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.18">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.35.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vyādhiviśeṣās tu prāg abhihitāḥ sarvvaṃ evaite trividhā bhavanti
                        | sādhyā yāpyāḥ pratyākhyeyāś ceti | tatra sādhya yāpya pratyākhye
                        yān vyādhīn bhūyatri vidhā parīkṣeta | kimayam aupasargikaḥ prāk
                        kevalo 'nyalakṣaṇa iti | taraupasargiko nāma yaḥ pūrvvotpannaṃ
                        vyādhiñ jaghanyakālajāto vyādhir upasṛjati | sa tat mūle sa
                        evopadravasaṃjñaḥ | prāk kevalo nāma | yaḥ prāgevotpanno vyādhirar
                        apūrvarūpopadravaś ca | anya lakṣaṇo nāma yo bhaviṣyat khyāpakaḥ
                        sa pūrvvarūpasaṃjñaḥ | tatra sopadravam anyonyāvirodhenopacaret |
                        valavantaram upadravam vā prāk kevalaṃ yathāsvam pratikurvīta |
                        anye lakṣaṇe tv ādivyādhau yathā yathāvat prayateta | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.24">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.35.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         prāg abhihito 'gnir annābhipācakaḥ sa pañcavidho bhavati || samo
                        doṣābhipanno vikriyām āpanna iti || viṣamo vātena | tīkṣṇa pittena
                        | mandaḥ śleṣmaṇā | samaḥ sarvvaiḥ samar iti || tatra yo yathā
                        kālam annam upayuktaṃ samya pacati sa samaḥ | yas tu kadācit
                        samyak pacati kadācid asamyak pacaty ādhmānaśūlātīsārapravāhaṇāni
                        kṛtvā pacati sa viṣamaḥ | yas tu prabhūtam apy annam upayuktam āśu
                        pacati sa tīkṣṇaḥ | sarvābhivardhamāno 'tyagnir bhavati || muhumr
                        mmuhuḥ prabhūtataram annam upayuktam āśutaraṃ pacati pākānte ca
                        galatālvoṣṭhapraśoṣadāhasantāpān janayati asyaiva bhasmaka iti
                        vyapadiśanti || yas tv alpam apy annam upayuktam
                        udaraśirogauravakāsaśvāsacchardiprasekagātrasadanāni kṛtvā mahā
                        kālena pacati sa mandaḥ || bha || </l>

                        kriyāviśeṣair upacaret || tīkṣṇam madhurasnigdhayuktair
                        vvirecanaiś ca | evam evāty agnim viśeṣeṇa māhiyaird
                        dadhikṣīrasarppibhir iti || mande kaṭutiktakaṣāyair vvamanaiś ca
                        || bha || </l>

                        tatronaṣoḍaśavarṣād vālābhavanti | te trividhāḥ kṣīrapāḥ
                        kṣīrānnādā annādā iti | ṣoḍaśasaptatyor antare madhyasvayas tasyad
                        vikalpo vṛddhir yauvanaṃ sampūrṇṇateti | tatrāviṃśater vṛddhir
                        ātriṃśato yauvanam ācatvāriṃśataḥ sarvvadhātvindriyasampūrṇṇetiti
                        || ata ūrdhvaṃ hā nir bhavati yāvadā saptateḥ | saptatyāsrūrdhaṃ
                        kṣīyamāṇadhātvindriyavalavīryotsāho 'nyahani valīpalitakhālity
                        akāsaśvāsaprabhṛtibhir upadravair abhibhūyamānaṃ
                        sarvvakriyāsvasamarthā jīrṇṇāgāram ivāvasīdati | tam vṛddham
                        ācakṣate | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.50">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.35.50</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ucite varttamānasya nāsti deśakṛtam bhayaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         āhārasvapnaceṣṭādau taddeśaḥ saguṇa satīti || </l>

                    <l ana="letter-numerals" xml:id="SS.1.35.trailer">ity adhyāya 35</l>

                            >miśrakannāmādhyāyaṃ</foreign>) which is located between

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.2"/>

                        <caesura/>
                         ahiṃsā caiva rāsnā ca pralepo vātaśophahā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.4">

                        <caesura/>
                         dūrvvā ca nalamūlañ ca madhukañ candanan tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         śītalāś ca gaṇāḥ sarvve pralepaḥ pittaśophahā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.37.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         āgantuje raktaje ca lepa eṣo 'bhipūjitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vidhirvviṣaghno viṣaje pittaghno 'bhihitas tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.6">

                        <caesura/>
                         eke ṣikājaśṛṅgī ca pralepaḥ śleṣmaśophahā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.37.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ete ca varggā lodhrañ ca pathyā piṇḍīkṛtāstuyaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         anantā ceti lepo 'yaṃ śophesarvvakṛtehitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.37.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         snigdho 'mlalavaṇo vāte koṣṇaḥ śītaḥ payoyutaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pitte 'thoṣṇeh kaphe kṣāramūtrāḍhyastatpraśāntaye || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.9">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.10ef">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.11">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.12">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.37.16ab"/>

                <div corresp="1.37 in NAK 5-333" n="36" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 37 (bhūmipravibhāgavijñānīyam) of the
                        Nepalese version, adhyāya 36 in the vulgate. Draft based on MS
                        H]</head>
                    <note xml:lang="en">There are large differences between the Ācārya
                        1931 and 1938 editions version of Cakrapāṇidatta's commentary on
                        this adhyāya.</note>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.36.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto bhūmipravibhāgavijñānīyam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.36.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         svabhraśarkkarāśmaviṣamavalmīkaśmaśānāghatadevatāyatanasikatoṣairar
                        anupahatāmanūṣarāmabhaṃgurāmadūrodakāṃ snigdhāṃ prarohavatīṃ
                        mṛdvīṃ sthirāṃ samāṃ gaurīṃ lohitāṃ vā bhūmim auṣadha grahaṇāya
                        parīkṣeta || tasyāṅ jātam api hi
                        krimaviṣaśastrātapapavanadahanatoyasambādhamārggair
                        anupahatamekasāraṃ puṣṭam avagāḍhamūlaṃ cauṣadhamādadyād ity eṣāṃ
                        bhūmiparīkṣāvibhāgaḥ sāmānyaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.36.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         viśeṣatas tu tatra aśmavatī sthirā gurvvī śdhāmā kṛṣṇā vā
                        sthūlatṛṇaśasyaprāyāḥ svaguṇabhūyiṣṭhā | snigdhā śītalāsannodakā
                        snigdhatṛṇaśasyākomalavṛkṣaprāyā śuklāmbuguṇabhūyiṣṭhā ||
                        nānāvarṇṇā laghvāśmavatī viralālyapāṇḍuraprarohāgniguṇabhūyiṣṭhā
                        || rūkṣā bhasmarāsabhavarṇṇā
                        kṣatanuvṛkṣakoṭarālparasaprāyānilaguṇabhūyiṣṭhā || mṛdvī
                        samāvyabhravatyavyaktarasajalā mahāparvvatavṛkṣaprāryā syāmā
                        cākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.36.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra kecid ācāryāḥ prāvṛṭvarṣāśaraddhemantavasantagrīṣmeṣu
                        yathāsaṃkhyam mūlapattratvacakṣīrasāraphalāny ādadīta || tat tu na
                        samyak kasmāt saumyāgneyatvāj jagataḥ | saumyāny auṣadhāni
                        saumyeṣv ṛtuṣv ādadīta | āgneyāny āgneyeṣv evam avyāpannāni
                        bhavanti || saumyāny auṣadhāni saumyeṣv ṛtuṣu gṛhītāni
                        somaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ bhūmau madhuratarāsnigdhatarāṇiśītatarāṇi
                        bhavanti | āgneyāny auṣadhāni āgneyeṣv ṛtuṣu
                        gṛhītānyagniguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ bhūmau uṣṇatarāṇi kaṭutarāṇi
                        rūkṣatarāṇi bhavanti | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.36.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrā pṛthivῑguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ bhūmau jātāni
                        virecanadravyāṇyādadīta | agnyanilaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāñ ca
                        vamanadravyāṇi | ubhayaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyām ubhayatobhāgaharāṇi |
                        ākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ saṃśamanāny evam balavattarāṇi bhavanti | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.36.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvvāṇi cābhinavānyatra madhughṛtapippalīviḍaṅgebhya iti || </l>

                    <l corresp="1.36.11 of 1938 ed" xml:id="SS.1.36.9"/>

                    <l corresp="1.36.12 of 1938 ed" xml:id="SS.1.36.10"/>

                    <l corresp="1.36.13 of 1938 ed" xml:id="SS.1.36.11"/>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         śeṣam anyat tv abhinavaṃ gṛhṇīyād doṣavarjjitaṃ || </l>

                    <l corresp="1.36.16 of 1938 ed" xml:id="SS.1.36.15">

                    <l corresp="1.36.17 of 1938 ed" xml:id="SS.1.36.16">

                        <caesura/>
                         plotamṛdbhāṇḍaphalakaṃ saṅkuvinyastabheṣajān |
                        <caesura/>
                         praśastāyān diśi śucau bheṣajāgāram iṣyate || </l>

                    <l corresp="1.36.10 of 1938 ed" xml:id="SS.1.36.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.36.8" corresp="1.36.10 of 1938
                            ed</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         gopālās tāpasā vyādhā ye cānye vanacāriṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mūlāhārāś ca ye teṣāṃ bheṣajavyaktir iṣyate iti || </l>

                <div n="38" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 38, draft based on MS H]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.38.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto dravyasaṅgrahaṇīyam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.38.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pañcatriṃśad dravyagaṇā bhavanti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.38.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tad yathā | vidārigandhā vidārīviśvadevā sahadevāśvadaṃṣṭrā
                        pṛthakparṇṇī śatāvarīe śārivā jīvakarṣabho kṣudrasahā bṛhatyau
                        punarnnaiveraṇḍahaṃsapādīvṛścikālyṛṣabhī śṛgālavinnā ceti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.38.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vidārigandhādirayaṅ gaṇaḥ pittānilāpahaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śophagulmāṅgamarddorddhvaśvāsakāsavināśanaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.38.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         āragvadhamadanaphalagopaghoṇṭākaṇṭakī
                        kaṇṭakārīkuṭajaphalapāṭhāpāṭalīmūrvvāsaptaparṇṇanimbakuraṇaaṭakaguḍūcīcitrakaśārṅgaṣṭādvikarañjapaṭolakirātatiktakāḥ
                        suṣavī ceti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.38.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         āragvadhādirity eṣa gaṇaḥ śleṣmaviṣāpahaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mehakuṣṭajvaravamīkaṇḍūghno vraṇaśodhanaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.8"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.9"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.10"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.11"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.12">śālasārājakarṇṇakhadirakramubhūrjjameṣaśṛṅgīti
                        nisacandanakucandanaśiṃśapā śirīṣāsanadhavārjjunanaktamālapūtīkāś
                        ca karṇṇagurūṇi kālīyakañ ceti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.13">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.38.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śālasārādir ity eṣa gaṇaḥ kuṣṭhavināśanaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         mehapāṇḍvāmayaharaḥ kaphamedoviśoṣaṇaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.13.1">
                        varuṇārttagalamadhuśigrutarkkārīmeṣaśṛṅgīpūtīkanaktamālapāṭalāgnimanthaśairīyakadvayaṃ
                        bimbīcitraśatāvarībilvājaśṛṅgīdarbbhābṛhatīdvayañ ceti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.13.2">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1.38.13.2</label>
                        <caesura/>

                <div n="39" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 39, draft based on MS H]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.39.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athātaḥ saṃśodhanasaṃśamanīyam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.39.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         madanakuṭajajīmūtakekṣvākudhāmārggavakṛtavedhanalodhrasarṣapaviḍaṅgapippalīkarañjaprapūnāḍakovidārāriṣṭāśvagandhāvidulabandhumadhukajīvantī
                        bimbīphalāmṛgervvāru citrasvetā
                        śalapuṣpīvacācetyūrddhvabhāgaharāṇi || tatra
                        kovidārapūrvvāṇāmphalāni | kovidārādīnām mūlāni ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.39.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tṛvṛcchyāmādantīdravantīsaphalāviṣāṇigavākṣīcchagalāntrīpīlusnehāsuvarṇṇakṣīrīcitrakakiṇihīkuśakāsatilvakampilyakarampakapāṭalā
                        pūgaharītakyāmalakavibhītakanīlinīpañcaṅgulapūtīkāragvadhamahāvṛkṣasaptacchadārkkareṇu
                        jyotiṣmatī cetyadhobhāgaharāṇi ||tatra tilvakapūrvvāṇāṃ mūlāni |
                        tilvakādīnām pāṭalyantānāñ ca tvacaḥ | pūgādīnām eraṇḍāntānām
                        phalāni | pūtīkāragvadhayoḥ patrāṇi | śeṣāṇāṃ kṣīrāṇīti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.39.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kośātakī saptalā devadālī karavallikā cety ubhayato bhāgaharāṇi |
                        eṣāṃ svarasāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.39.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pippalīviḍaṅgāpāmārggaśigruśirīṣasiddhārthakamaricakaravīrabimbīgirikarṇṇikākiṇihīvacājyotiṣmatīkarañjārkkalaśunātiviṣāśṛ
                        ṅgaveratālīsatamālasurasārjjakeṅgudīmeṣaśṛṅgīmātuluṅgīmuruṅgīpīlujātīsālatālamadhūkalākṣāhiṃgulavaṇamadyagośakṛdrasomūtrāṇi
                        śirovirecanāni | tatra karavīrapūrvvāṇām phalāni | tālīsapūrvvāṇāṅ
                        kandāḥ | tālīsakādīnāmarjjakāntānām patrāṇi | iṅgudīmeṣaśṛṅgyos
                        tvak | mātuluṅgīmuruṅgīpīlujātīnām puṣpāṇi | śālatālamadhūkānāṃ
                        sārāḥ | lākṣāhiṃgu ca niryāsau | lavaṇāni pārthivaviśeṣāḥ | madyam
                        āsutasaṃyogāḥ | śakṛdrasamūtre malāviti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.39.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         saṃśamanāni ata urdhvvam vakṣyāmaḥ || tatra
                        bhadradārukuṣṭhaharidrāvaruṇameṣaśṛṅgībalātibalārttagalakacchurāśallakīkuberākṣīvīratarasahacarāgnimanthavatsādanīśva
                        daṃṣṭrāśmabhedakārkkālarkkaśatāvarīpunarnnavāsukavasirakāñcanabhārggīvṛścikālīvadarayavakulattaprabhṛtīni
                        dve cādye pañcamūlyau samāsena vātasaṃ śamano varggaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.39.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         candanahrīverośīramañjiṣṭhāpayasyāgundraśevālakahlārakotpalamūrvvāprabhṛtīni
                        nyagrodhādirutpalādiriti samāsena pittasaṃśamano vargaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.39.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kāleyakāgurutailaparṇṇikākuṣṭhaharidrāśītaśivāśatapuṣpāsaralārāsnāprakīryodakīceṅgudīsumanāḥ
                        kākādanīlāṅgalakīhastiparṇṇamuñjālalāmajja
                        kaprabhṛtīnivallīkaṇṭakapañcamūlyau dve pippalyādir mmuṣkakādir
                        vvacādiḥ surasādirāragvadhādir utpalādir iti samāsena
                        śleṣmasaṃśamano varggaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.39.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra sarvvāṇy evauṣadhāni vyādhagnipuruṣabalānyevekṣya vidadhyād
                        vyādhyabalād adhikam auṣadham upayuktan tam upasāmyavyādhim
                        anyamāvahati || agnyabalād adhikam ajīrṇṇam viṣṭabhya vā pacyate |
                        puruṣabalād adhikaṃ glānimūrcchanā vahati | śamanam evaṃ
                        saṃśodhanam atipātayati | hīnam ebhyo dattam akiñcitkaram bhavati
                        | tasmāt samam eva vidhyāt ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.39.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavati cātra ||
                        <caesura/>
                         roge śodhanasādhye tu yam vidyād doṣam ulvanaṃ
                        <caesura/>
                         taṃ samīkṣya bhiṣak kuryād doṣapacyāvanaṃ mṛduḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.11.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1.39.11.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         jaloddhṛtauṣadhapalas toyadvikuḍavāyutaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pādāvaśeṣitaḥ kvāthaḥ pūtaḥ pānāya śasyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.39.11.2">

                        <caesura/>

                <div n="40" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 40, draft based on MS H]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.40.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto dravyarasavīryavipākavijñānīyam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.40.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kecid ācāryā vruvate | dravyam pradhānam kasmāt vyavasthitatvāt |
                        iha khalu dravyam vyavasthitan na rasādayaḥ | yathā ye phale
                        rasādayas te pakve na bhavanti || nityatvāc ca nityaṃ hi dravyam
                        anityaṃ hi guṇāḥ | yathā kalkādi pravibhāgās tad eva
                        sampannarasagandhaṃ vyāpannarasagandhavān bhavatīti |
                        svajātivyavasthānāc ca yathā pārthivaṃ dravyam anyabhāvan na
                        gacchati | evaṃ śoṣāṇi | pañcendriyagrahaṇāc ca | pañcaindriyair
                        gṛhyate draṣṭavyan na rasādayaḥ | āśrayatvāc ca dravyam āśritārasā
                        iti | ārambha sāmarthyāc ca dravyāśrita ārambhaḥ || yathā
                        vidārigandhādim āhṛtyāv adya vipaced ity evam ādiṣu na rasādiṣ
                        ārambhaḥ | śāstraprāmāṇyāc ca śāstraṃ ha | dvividhan dravyaṃ
                        sthāvarañ jañgam ti | kramāpekṣikatvāc ca rasādīnāṃ rasādayo hi
                        dravyakramam apekṣante yathā taruṇe taruṇāḥ | saṃpūrṇa sampūrṇā
                        iti | ekadeśasādhyatvāc ca dravyāṇām ekadeśenāpi vyādhayaḥ
                        sādhyante | yathā mahāvṛkṣakṣīreṇeti | tasmād dravyam pradhānan
                        rasādayaḥ kasmāt niravayavatvāt dravyasya | dravyalakṣaṇan tu
                        kriyāguṇasamavāyaḥ kriyādravye vidyate | guṇāḥ samavāyakāraṇañ
                        ceti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.40.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nety āhur anye rasās tu pradhānan kasmāt āgamāt āgamo hi śāstram
                        ity ucyate | śāstre rasā adhikṛtā yathā rasāyatta āhāra iti |
                        upadeśāc ca | upadiśyate hi | yathā madhurāmlalavaṇā vātaṃ
                        śamayanti | ato rasāḥ pradhānaṃ | anumāc ca | rasato hy anumīyate
                        dravyaṃ | yathā madhuram iti || ṛṣivacanāc ca | ṛṣivacano vedaḥ |
                        yathā kiñcid ījyārtham madhuram āhared iti | tasmāt rasāḥ
                        pradhānaṃ | raseṣu tu guṇasaṃjñā rasalakṣaṇam atropadekṣyāmaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.40.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nety āhur anye vīryam pradhānam iti | kasmāt prādhānyāt |
                        ihatvauṣadhakarmmāṇi vīrya prādhānyaṃ na bhavanti | tad yathā |
                        urddhabhāgodhobhāgobhayabhāgasaṃśamanaṃ
                        sāṅgrāhikadīpanalekhanavṛṃhaṇarasāyanavājīkaraṇaś ca
                        yathuharavilayanadāraṇamarddanaprāṇaghnaviṣapraśamanāni vīrya
                        prādhānyena bhavanti | tantu vīryaṃ dvividhaṃ | uṣṇaṃ śītaṃ
                        cāgniṣomīyatvāj jagataḥ | kecid aṣṭavidham āhuḥ | uṣṇaṃ śītaṃ
                        snigdhaṃ rūkṣam vi ṣadam piccilam mṛdus tīkṣṇañ ceti | etāni khalu
                        vīryāṇi svabhāvaguṇotkarṣād rasam abhibhūyātmakarmma kurvvanti |
                        yathā tāvad vṛhatyañ ca mūlaṅ kaṣāya tiktaṃ vātaṃ śamayaty
                        uṣṇavīryatvāt | kaṭukā pippalīpittaṃ śamayati | mṛduśītavīryatvāt
                        | tiktā kākamācī pittaṃ varddhayaty uṣṇavīryatvāt | kaṭukaṃ mūlaṃ
                        śleṣmāṇaṃ varddhayati snigdhavīryatvāt | amlaṃ kapitthaṃ śleṣmāṇaṃ
                        ti rukṣavīryatvāt || bha || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.40.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ye rasā vātaśamanā bhavanti yadi teṣu vai |
                        <caesura/>
                         rukṣalāghavaśaity āni na te hanyuḥ samīraṇam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.40.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ye rasāḥ pittaśamanā bhavanti yadi teṣuvai |
                        <caesura/>
                         taikṣṇyauṣṇyalaghutā caiva na te talkarmmakāriṇaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.40.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ye rasāḥ śleṣmaśamanā bhavanti yadi teṣu vai |
                        <caesura/>
                         snehagauravaśaity ānu na te tatkarmmakāriṇaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.40.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmād vīryaṃ pradhānam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.40.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nety āhur anye vipākaḥ pradhānam iti | kasmāt samyaṅ mithyā
                        vipakvatvāt | iha hi dravyāṇyapaha tāni samyaṅ mithyā cāvipakvāni
                        guṇan doṣam vā janayaṃti | tatrāhur anye prati ra sampāka iti |
                        vipākaḥ kecit trividham icchanti | madhuram amlam kaṭukañceti |
                        tat tu na samyak | bhūtaguṇād āgamāc cāmlo vipāko nāsti | pittaṃ
                        hi vidagdham amlatām upaity āgneyatvāt | yad evaṃ lavaṇo 'pyanyaḥ
                        pāke bhaviṣyati | śleṣmā hi vidagdho lavaṇatām upaiti |
                        tamādasiddhānta eṣaḥ | pratirasam amlāmlasyaivaṃ sarvvaṣām iti
                        dṛṣṭāntañ codāharanti | yathā śāliyavamudgādayaḥ prakīrṇāḥ
                        svabhāvam uttarakāle pi na parity ajanti tadvat iti | kecit punar
                        avalavanto valavatāṃ vaśamāyānt it evam avasthitaḥ pāka iti |
                        āgame svāha | dvividha eva pāko madhuraḥ kaṭukaś ca | tayor
                        madhurākhyo guruḥ kaṭukākhyo laghur iti | tatra
                        pṛthivyaptejovāyvākāśānāṃ dvaividhyam bhavati | guṇasādharmyān
                        gurutā | laghutā ca pṛthivyā yo gurvyaḥ | śeṣāṇi laghūni tasmād
                        dvividha eva pāko bhavati || bha ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.40.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dravyeṣu pacyamāneṣu yeṣv ambupṛthivīguṇāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nivarttante 'dhikās tatra pāko madhura ucyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.12">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.13">

                         pṛthak tvavādināmeṣeva vādinām vādasaṃgrahaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         caturṇṇām api sāmagryam icchantyatra vipaścitaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.14">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.40.14</label>

                         tad dravyam ātmanā kiñcit kiñcid vīryeṇa sevitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.15">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.16">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.17">

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         raseṣu na bhavantyete nirguṇāḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.18">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.40.18</label>
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.19">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.40.19</label>

                        <caesura/>
                         āgamenopayojyāni bheṣajāni vicakṣaṇaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.20">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.40.20</label>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.21">

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.41.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto dravyaviśeṣavijñānīyam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.41.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra pṛthivyaptejovāyvākāśānāṃ samudāyād dravyābhinirvṛttir
                        bbhavati | idaṃ pārthivam idam apyam idan tejasam idam vāyavyam
                        idam ākāśyam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1.41.4.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra sthūla<pc> </pc>sāndra<pc> </pc>manda<pc
                            > </pc>sthira<pc> </pc>guru<pc> </pc>kaṭhina<pc
                            > </pc>gaṃdha<pc> </pc>guṇa<pc> </pc>bahulam īṣatkaṣāyaprāyaso
                        madhuram iti pārthivan tat sthairya<pc> </pc>gaurava<pc
                            > </pc>saṃghātopacaya<pc> </pc>karaṃ viśeṣataś
                        cādhogatisvabhāvam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.2">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1.41.4.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śīta<pc> </pc>stimita<pc> </pc>manda<pc> </pc>guru<pc> </pc>rasa<pc> </pc>sāndra<pc> </pc>mṛdu<pc> </pc>picchila<pc> </pc>rasa<pc> </pc>guṇa<pc> </pc>bahulam
                        īṣadamlaṃ prāyaso madhuram āpyan tat snehanahlādanaviṣyandanakaram
                        iti | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1.41.4.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tīkṣṇoṣṇarūkṣasūkṣmalaghuviṣadaṃ rūpaguṇabahulam īṣadamlaprāyam
                        viśeṣataś corddhvagatisvabhāvam iti taijasaṃ ||
                        taddahanapacanatāpanaprakāśanaprabhāvarṇṇakaram iti | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1.41.4.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sūkṣmarūkṣakharaśiśiralaghuviṣadaṃ sparśaguṇabahulam īṣattiktam
                        viśeṣataḥ kaṣāyam iti vāyavyaṃ tadvaiṣadyaṃ
                        lāghavaglapanavirūkṣaṇakaram iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1.41.4.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ślakṣṇasūkṣmavyavāyiviṣadaviviktarasaṃ śabdaguṇabahulam ākāśyan
                        tasmāt tat mārddavasauṣiryalāghavakaram iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.41.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         anena nidarśanena nānauṣadhabhūtañ jagati kiñcid dravyam astīti
                        kṛtvā tan taṃ yuktiviśeṣamarthañ cābhipratītya svavīryaguṇayuktāni
                        dravyāṇi kārmmukāni<anchor n="SS.1.41.5-n1"/> bhavanti || tāni
                        yadā kurvvanti sa kālaḥ | yat kurvanti tat karmma | yena kurvvanti
                        tad vīryaṃ | yatra kurvvanti tad adhikaraṇaṃ | yathā kurvvanti sa
                        upāyaḥ | yad abhiniṣpādayanti tat phalam iti | </l>
                    <ab corresp="#SS.1.41.5" type="apparatus">
                        <list type="notes">
                            <item xml:lang="en" corresp="#SS.1.41.5-n1">The word
                                    <foreign>kārmuka</foreign> is known in early medical
                                texts from this instance and one in the
                                    <title>Carakasaṃhitā</title> 1.26.13. The word is
                                formed by P.5.1.103 in the sense “capable of accomplishing
                                an action."</item>
                        </list>
                    </ab>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.41.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tad atra virecanadravyāṇy ambupṛthivīguṇabhūyiṣṭhāni | pṛthivyāpo
                        hi gurvvyaḥ | gurutvād adho gacchanti | tasmād virecanadravyāṇy
                        ambupṛthivīguṇabhūyiṣṭhāni | vamanadravyāṇy
                        agnivāyuguṇabhūyiṣṭhāni | agnivāyū hi laghū laghutvāc corddhvam
                        uttiṣṭhataḥ | tasmād vamanaprāmāṇyād agnivāyubhūyiṣṭhāny
                        ubhayaguṇabhūyiṣṭhan dravyam ubhayato bhāgaharaṃ |
                        ākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ saṃśamanaṃ | sāṃgrāhikam anilaguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ |
                        dīpanam agniguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ | lekhanam anilānalaguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ |
                        bṛṃhanam pṛthivyambuguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ | evam auṣadhakarmmāṇy anumānāt
                        sādhayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.41.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavanti ślokāḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         mahyambvagnyātmakair ddravyais tribhiḥ sāmyati mārutaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         khabhūmyambuvāyujaiḥ pittañ caturbbhiḥ saṃpraśāmyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.41.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphaḥ khatejo'nilajais tribhiḥ śāmyati dehināṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         khavāyuktābhyān dravyābhyāṃ vṛddhim abhyeti mārutaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.41.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         āgneyam eva yad dravyan tena pittam udīryate |
                        <caesura/>
                         mahyambujābhyān dravyābhyāṅ kaphaś cābhivivarddhate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.41.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         evam eva guṇādhikyaṃ dravye dravye vyavasthitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dviśo vā bahuśo vāpi jñātvā doṣe 'vacācaret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.41.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra ya ime guṇāṣṭauvīryasaṃjñakāḥ |
                        śītoṣṇasnigdharūkṣamṛdutīkṣṇapicchilaviṣadās teṣān tīkṣṇoṣṇāv
                        āgneyau | śītapicchilāv ambuguṇabhūyiṣṭhau |
                        pṛthivīsomaguṇabhūyiṣṭhaḥ | snehas toyākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ |
                        mṛdutvaṃ | vāyuguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ raukṣyaṃ | kṣitisamīraṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ
                        vaiṣadyaṃ | vipākāv uktaguṇau | karmmāṇy uṣṇasya
                        dahanapācanamūrcchanasvedanavamanavirecanāni || śītasya
                        prahlādanaviṣkambhanasthirīkaraṇaprasādanakledanajīvanāni |
                        snigdhasya snehanabṛṃhaṇasantarppaṇavyājīkaraṇavayaḥsthāpanāni ||
                        rūkṣasyānilavṛddhisaṃgrahaṇapīḍanavirūkṣaśoṣarohaṇāni || viṣadasya
                        kledāvūṣaṇavirūkṣaśoṣarohaṇāni ||
                        picchilasyopalepanapūraṇabṛṃhaṇasaṃśleṣaṇavyājīkaraṇāni || mṛdo
                        raktamān saprasādanamukhyasaṃsparśanāni || tīkṣṇasya
                        saṅgrahācūṣaṇāvadāraṇaśrāvaṇāni | tatroṣṇasnigdhau vātaghnau |
                        śītamṛdupicchilāḥ pittaghnāḥ | tīkṣṇarūkṣaviṣadāḥ śleṣmaghnāḥ |
                        gurupāko vātapittaghnaḥ | laghupākaḥ śleṣmapittaghna iti | teṣu
                        mṛduśītoṣṇāḥ sparśagrāhyāḥ | picchilaviṣadau cakṣuḥsparśābhyāṃ |
                        snigdharūkṣau cakṣuṣā | tīkṣṇaḥ sukhaduḥkhotpādanāt | gurupākaḥ
                        sṛṣṭaviṇmūtratayā kaphāṃ kleśanañ ca | laghur bbaddhaviṇmūtratayā
                        mārutakopanañ ca | tatra tulyaguṇeṣu bhūteṣu rasavaiśeṣyam
                        upalakṣayet || yathā madhuro guruś ca pārthivaḥ |
                        madhurasnigdhaśītāś cāpyā iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.12">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.41.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         || bhavati cātra || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.12i">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1.41.12i</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         guṇā ye uktā dravyeṣu śarīreṣv api tān viduḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sthānavṛddhikṣayāt tasmād dehināṃ dravyahetukā iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.trailer"> || 41 ||</l>
                </div>
                <div n="42" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 42, draft based on MS H]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.42.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto rasaviśeṣavi-jñānīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.42.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ākāśapavanadahanatoyabhūmiṣu yathāsaṅkhyam ekottaraparivṛddhāḥ ||
                        śa bdasparśarūparasagandhāḥ || tasmād āpyo rasaḥ
                        parasparānupraveśāc ca sarvveṣāṃ sānnidhyam asti utkarṣāt tu
                        grahaṇaṃ | sa khalvāpyo rasaḥ śeṣabhūtasaṃsarggādvidagdhaḥ
                        ṣaḍvidho bhavati | tad yathā | madhuro 'mlo lavaṇaḥ kaṭukastiktaḥ
                        kaṣāya iti | tatrodakavāhulyātmadhuraḥ | toyāgnivāhulyādamlaḥ
                        bhūmyagnivāhulyāl lavaṇaḥ vāyvākāśavāhulyāttiktaḥ |
                        vāyvagnivāhulyātkaṭukaḥ pṛthivyanilavāhulyātkaṣāya iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.42.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra madhurāmlalavaṇā vātaghnāḥ | madhuratiktakaṣāyāḥ pittaghnāḥ
                        kaṭutiktakaṣāyāḥ śleṣmaghnāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.42.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra vāyurātmaivātmā | pittamāgneyaṃ | śleṣma saumya iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.42.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ta ete rasāḥ svayonivardhanā anyayonipraśamanāś ca | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.42.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kecid āhur agnīṣomīyatvājjagataḥ | dvividhā rasāḥ saumyā āgneyāś
                        ca | tatra madhuratiktakaṣāyāḥ saumyāḥ dvividhā kaṭvamlalavaṇā
                        āgneyāḥ | madhurāmlalavaṇāḥ snigdhā guravaś ca dvividhā
                        kaṭutiktakaṣāyā rūkṣā laghavaś ca | saumyāḥ śītāḥ | āgneyās tūṣṇāḥ
                        | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.8.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1.42.8.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra śaityarūkṣalāghavavaiṣadyaguṇalakṣaṇo vāyuḥ | tasya
                        samānayoniḥ kaṣāyo rasaḥ | saumyaḥ śaityāc chaity am
                        abhivardhayati | raukṣyād raukṣyaṃ lāghavāl lāghavaṃ vaiṣadyād
                        vaiṣadyam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.8.2">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1.42.8.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         auṣṇyataikṣṇyaraukṣyalāghavavaiṣadyaguṇalakṣaṇampittantasya
                        samānayoniḥ kaṭuko rasaḥ | saumya auṣṇyād auṣṇyam abhivardhayati |
                        taikṣṇyāt taikṣṇyaṃ raukṣyād raukṣyaṃ lāghavāl lāghavaṃ vaiśadyād
                        vaiśadyam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.8.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1.42.8.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mādhuryasnehagauravaśaityapaicchilyaguṇalakṣaṇaḥ śleṣmā tasya
                        samānayo nirmadhuro rasaḥ | saumya mādhuryāt mādhuryam
                        abhivardhayati | snehāt snehaṃ gauravād gauravaṃ śaityāc chaityaṃ
                        paicchilyāt paicchilyam iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.42.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya punar vviparītaḥ kaṭuko rasaḥ | śleṣmaṇaḥ pratyanīkatvāt |
                        kaṭukyātmādhuryam abhibhavati | raukṣyāt snehaṃ lāghavād gauravaṃ
                        auṣṇyāt paicchity an tad etan nidarśanamātram uktaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.42.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rasalakṣaṇam ata ūrdhvaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ || tatra yaḥ paritoṣam
                        utpādayati tarppayati mukhopalepañ janayati prahlādayati śleṣmāṇañ
                        cābhivardhayati sa madhuraḥ || yo dantaharṣam utpādayati |
                        mukhāśrāvañ jana-yati śraddhāñ cotpādayati so 'mlaḥ || yo
                        bhaktarucim utpādayati | kaphaprasekañ janayati mārddavañ
                        copādayati sa lavaṇaḥ || yo jihvām udvejayati śiro gṛhṇāti nāsikāñ
                        ca śrāvayati sa kaṭukaḥ || yo gale śoṣam utpāda-yati
                        mukhavaiṣadyam utpādayati bhaktaruciñ copādyati sa tiktaḥ || ya
                        āsyam pariśoṣayati- jihvāṃ stambhayati kaṇṭham badhnāti hṛdayam
                        pīḍayati sa kaṣāyaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1.42.10.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rasaguṇān ata ūrdhvam vakṣyāmaḥ || tatra madhuro raso
                        raktamāṃsado 'sthimajjojaḥ śukravardhanaś cākṣuṣyaḥ
                        keśyauvalakṛtsandhānaḥ śoṇitaḥ śoṇitaprasādo
                        vālavṛddhakṣatakṣīṇahitaḥ ṣaṭpadapipīlikānāmiṣṭatamaḥ ||
                        tṛṣṇāmūrcchādāhaḥ praśamanaḥ | ṣaḍindriyaprasādanaś ceti | sa
                        evaṃguṇo 'py eka evātyartham upayujyamānaḥ kāsaḥ śvāso
                        lasakavamathurvvadanamādhuryasvaropaghātakṛmigalagaṇḍān āpādayati
                        | tathārvvudaślīpadabastigudopalepābhiṣyandaprabhṛtīn
                        nayanavikārānn upajayati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.2">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1.42.10.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         amlas tu jaraṇaḥ pācanapavananigrahaṇo nulomano vidāhī vahiḥśītaḥ
                        kledanaḥ prāyaśo hṛdyaś ceti | sa khalv evaṃguṇo 'py eka
                        evātyartham upayujyamāno
                        dantaharṣanayanasammīlanaromasamvejanakaphavilāyanaśarīrapraśithilatām
                        āpādayati | tathā
                        kṣatavihatadagdhadaṣṭabhagnaśū-nacyutāvamathitacchiyavisarppitacchinnaviddhotpiṣṭādīni
                        pāca-yaty āgneyasvabhāvatvvāt || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1.42.10.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         lavaṇas tu saṃśodhanaḥ pācano viśleṣaṇas tarppaṇaḥ kledanaḥ
                        śaithilyakṛt sarvvarasapratyanīkabhūto mārggaviśodhanaḥ
                        sarvvaśarīrāvayavamārddavakaraś ceti | sa khalu evaṃguṇo 'py eka
                        evātyartham upasevyamāno gātrakaṇḍūko tha śophavaivarṇṇakaraḥ
                        svaropaghātendriyopatāpān upajanayati |
                        tathākṣimukhapākaraktapittavātaśoṇitāmlīkāprabhṛtīnvikārān
                        upajanayati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1.42.10.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṭukas tu dīpanaḥ pācano rocanaḥ śodhanaḥ sthaulyā
                        lyālasakaviṣakuṣṭhakaṇḍūpraśamanaḥ sandhibandhacchedano vasādanas
                        stanyaśukrakaphamedasām upahantā ceti | sa khalv evaṃguṇo 'py eka
                        evātyartham upayujyamāno bhramamadagalatālvoṣṭhaśoṣadāhasantāpān
                        āpādayati | tathā valavighātakampatodabhedakṛt
                        karacaraṇapārśvapṛṣṭhaprabhṛtiṣu ca vātaśūlān upajanayati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1.42.10.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tiktas tu rocano dīpanaḥ śodhanaḥ kaṇḍūkoṣṭhatṛṣṇāmūrcchāpraśanaḥ
                        stanyaśodhano viṇmūtrakledamedovasāpūyopaśoṣaṇaś ceti | sa khalv
                        evaṅguṇo 'py eka evātyartham upayujyamāno
                        gātramanyāstambhākṣepakordditaśiraḥśūlān upa-janayati | tathā
                        bhramatodabhedacchedāsyavairasyāny āpādayati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1.42.10.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṣāyas tu saṅgrāhiko ropaṇaḥ stambhanaḥ śodhanollekhanaḥ śoṣaṇaḥ
                        pīḍanaḥ kledopaśoṣaṇaś ceti | sa khalv evaṅguṇo 'py eka
                        evātyartham upayujyamāno
                        hṛdayapīḍāsyaśoṣodarādhmānavākyagrahamanyāstambhaprabhṛtīn vikārān
                        upajanayati | tathā
                        gātrasphuraṇacimicimāyanākuñcanākṣepaṇaprabhṛtīn
                        vikārānupajanayati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.42.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sarvveṣām eva dravyāṇy upadekṣyāmaḥ | tad yathā kākolyādi
                        kṣīraghṛtavasāmajjaśāliyavagodhūmamāṣaśṛṅgāṭakakaśeruka
                        kālāṅkālukapiyālapuṣkaravījakāśmaryamadhūkadrākṣākharjūrarājādananālikerekṣuvikārāḥ
                        |
                        balātibalātmaguptāvidārīpayasyāgokṣurakakṣīramoraṭamadhūlikākūṣmāṇḍādiḥ
                        samāsena madhuro varggaḥ ||
                        dāḍimāmalakamātuluṅgāmrāmrātakakapitthakaramarddavadaraprācīnāmalakakośāmrabhavyapārāvatavetraphalatintiḍīkalajacāmlavetasadantaśaṭhadadhitakrasurāsauvīratuṣodakadhānyāmlaprabhṛtīni
                        samāsenāmlo varggaḥ ||
                        saindhavasauvarccalaviḍapākyaromakasāmudrapācimakṣāroṣarasuvarccilaprabhṛtīni
                        samāsena lavaṇo varggaḥ || pippa-lyādiḥ surasādir
                        mmadhuśigrumūlakalaśunasumukhaśītaśivakuṣṭhadevadāruhareṇukā
                        'valgujaphalacaṇḍāguggulumustalāṅgalakīśukanāsīpīluprabhṛtī-ni
                        śālasārādiś ca prāyaśaḥ kaṭuko varggaḥ ||
                        āragvadhādirgguḍūcyādirmmaṇḍūkaparṇṇīvetrakarīraharidrādvayendrayavavaruṇasvādukaṇṭakasaptaparṇṇavṛhatīdvayaśaṃkhinītṛvṛtkṛtavedhanakarkkoṭakakāravellavārttākukaravīrasumanāḥśaṃkhapuṣpyapāmārggatrāyamāṇāśokarohivaijayantīsuvarccalāvṛścikālījyotiṣmatīprabhṛtīni
                        tikto varggaḥ || nyagrodhādirambaṣṭhādir lodhrādiḥ
                        priyaṅvādistriphalā śallakījamvvasthitindukādīni katakaśākaphalāni
                        sālasārādiś ca prāyasaḥ
                        kuravakakovidārajīvantīsuniṣaṇṇakaprabhṛtīni varakādayo mudgādayaś
                        ca samāsena kaṣā-yo varggaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.12">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.42.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatraiteṣāṃ rasānāṃ saṃyogās triṣaṣṭirv bhavanti || tad yathā
                        pañcadaśa dvikāḥ | viṃśatis trikāḥ | pañcadaśa catuṣkāḥ | ṣaṭ
                        pañcakāḥ | ekaṣaṭkāḥ | ekaikaśaś ca śaḍrasā iti | teṣām anyatra
                        vakṣyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.13">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.42.13</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavati cātra ||
                        <caesura/>
                         yuktāḥ ṣaḍadhigacchanti valino vaśyatāṃ rasāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathā doṣāḥ prakupitā vaśaṃ yānti valīyasa iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.trailer"> || 42 ||</l>
