                <div n="43" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 43, draft based on MS H]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.43.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto vamanadravyavikalpavijñānīyam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.3.part1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1.43.3.part1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vamanadravyānām phalākhyānām madhye madanaphalāni śreṣṭhatamāni
                        bhavanti || tatra madanapuṣpāṇām ātapaśuṣkāṇā cūrṇaprakuñcaṃ
                        pratyak puṣpīnimvakaṣāyāṇām anyatamenālo pāyayitvā vāmayet |
                        madanaśatvāṭūcūrṇṇāny evam madhulavaṇayuktāny abhiprataptāni |
                        madanaśalāṭucūrṇṇasiddhām vā tilayavāgūn | nivṛttām vā nātihariti
                        pāṇḍūnāṃ kuśamūḍhāvavaddhamṛdgomayapraliptānāṃ
                        yavavūsamāṣaśālyādidhānyarāśāvaṣṭharātroṣitaklinnabhinnānām
                        phalapippalīrāhṛtyātape pariśoṣayet tāsāṃ
                        dadhipalavimṛditapariśuṣkāṇāṃ subhājanasthānām antarnnakhamuṣṭhim
                        uṣṇena yaṣṭhīmadhukaṣāyeṇa kovidārādhyanyatamakāṣāyeṇa vā vimṛdya
                        trirātraparyuṣitam madhusaindhavayuktam āśīrbhir abhimantritam
                        udaṅmukhaḥ prāṅmukham āturam pāyayet anena mantreṇa abhimantrya
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.3.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1.43.3.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         brahmadakṣāśvirūdrendrabhūcandrārkkānilānalāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ṛṣayaḥ sauṣadhigrāmā bhūtasaṃghāś ca pāntu te ||<anchor
                            n="SS.1.43.3.1-n1"/>
                    </l>
                    <ab corresp="#SS.1.43.3.1" type="apparatus">
                        <list type="Testimonia">
                            <item xml:lang="en" corresp="#SS.1.43.3.1-n1">This and the
                                next passage are found in the <title>Agnipurāṇa</title>
                                279.014cd (Mitra 1870: v.3, p.35).</item>
                        </list>
                    </ab>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.3.2">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1.43.3.2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         rasāyaneva siddhānān devānām amṛtaṃ yathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         sudhevottamanāgānāsbhaiṣajyam idam astu te ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.3.part2">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1.43.3.part2</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         viśeṣeṇa śleṣmajvarapratiśyāyāntarvvidradhiṣv apravarttamāne doṣe
                        pippalīvacāsarṣapakalkonmiśrair uṣṇāmvubhiḥ punaḥ punaḥ
                        pravarttayed āsamyag vāntalakṣaṇād iti | madanaphalamajjacūrṇṇam
                        vā tat kvāthaparibhāvitam vasena dravyakaṣāyeṇa | madanaphalamajjā
                        siddham vā payaḥ | madanaphalamajjasiddhena vā payasā vā yavāgūm
                        adhobhāgāsṛhṛdrogayoḥ | madanaphalamajjasiddhasya vā payaso
                        dadhibhāvam upagatasya | dadhyuttarakaṃ dadhi vā
                        kaphaprasekaśarddistameṣu | madanaphalamajjācūrṇṇa rasam vā
                        bhallātakasenhavadādāya phāṇitībhūtaṃ lehayet | ātapaśuṣkam vā
                        jīvantī kaṣāyeṇa pittakaphasthānagate | madanaphala majjākvātham
                        vā pippalyādi prativāpaṃ ūṣaṇanimvakaṣāya yor anyatamena
                        santarppaṇaṃ | kaphasarvvavyādhiharam iti madanaphalam uktaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.43.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         jīmūtakakusumacūrṇṇam vā pūrvvavad eva kṣīreṇa nivṛtteṣu yavāgūṃ
                        romaseṣu | santānikām vā nirllomaśeṣu | dadhyuttarakaṃ
                        haritakapāṇḍuṣu | dadhi tat kaṣāyasaṃsṛṭāṃ surām vā paryāgateṣu |
                        madanaphalamajja </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.43.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vidhānavat kuṭajaphalamajjavidhānaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.6"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.43.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ikṣvākukusumacūrṇṇam vā pūrvvavad eva kṣīreṇa | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.43.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dhāmārgavasyāpi madanaphalamajjā vidhānavad upayogaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.43.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kṛtavedhanamadanaphalamajjapippalīmām vamanadravyaparibhāvitānām
                        bahuśaś cūrṇṇam utpalādiṣu dattam āghrā ya vasati
                        tattvanavavaddhadoṣeṣu yavāgūmākaṇṭham pītavatsu ca dadyād iti |
                        śirovirecanāny evaṃ pradhānatamāni bhavanti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.10"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.43.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavati cātra
                        <caesura/>
                         kalkaiḥ kaṣāyaiḥ svarasaiś ca cūrṇṇair api ca vuddhimān |
                        <caesura/>
                         peyalehyādibhojyeṣu vamanānyūpakalpayet || </l>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>
                         pibet tad amlair anilādhijuṣṭaḥ ||</l>

                        ||</l>

                        |

                        saindhavañ ca ||</l>

                        tu |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.90">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.44.90</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ghṛteṣu taileṣu payaḥsu cāpi madyeṣu mūtreṣu tathā raseṣu |
                        <caesura/>
                         anneṣu bhakṣyeṣu tathaiva lehe virecanaṃ sādhu niyojanīya</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.44.91"/>

                <div n="45" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 45, draft based on MS H]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto dravadravyaviśeṣavijñānīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.2"/>
                    <!-- <lg type="varga"> -->
                    <p ana="subheading" style="bold">[Pānīyavarga]</p>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pānīyaṃm āntarīkṣyam anirddeśyarasam amṛtaṃ jīvanan tarppaṇan
                        dhāraṇam āśvāsajananaṃ śramaklamapipāsāmadamūrcchātandrāpraśamanam
                        ekāntataḥ pathyatamañ ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tad evāvanau patitam anyatamam upalabhyate |
                        nadīsarastaḍāgakūpavāpīpraśravaṇodbhijacauṇṭyādiṣu sthāneṣv
                        anyatamaṃ rasam upabhate | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra lohitakapilapāṇḍupītanīlaśukleṣv avanipradeśeṣu
                        madhurāmlalavaṇakaṭutiktakaṣāyā yathāsaṃkhyam udakarasā bhavantīty
                        eke bhāṣante || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.6">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.6</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tat tu na samyak pṛthivyādīnām anyo 'nyānupraveśakṛtaḥ sa
                        khalūdakaraso bhavaty utkarṣāpakarṣakṛtena saṃyogaviśeṣeṇa ||
                        tatra svalakṣaṇodakaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyām madhuraṃ |
                        toyāgniguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyām amlaṃ| pṛthivyagniguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ lavaṇaṃ
                        | vāyvagniguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṅ kaṭukaṃ| vāyvākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ
                        tiktaṃ | pṛthivyanilaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṅ kaṣāyaṃ |
                        ākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyām avyaktarasam avyaktaṃ hy ākāśam ity atas tat
                        pradhānam avyaktarasatvāt tat peyam āntarīkṣālābhe | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatrānta-rikṣañ caturvvidhaṃ || tadyāthā | dhāraṃ kāraṃ tauṣāraṃ
                        haimam iti | teṣān dhāraṃ pradhānaṃ laghutvāt tat punar dvividhaṃ
                        | gāṅgaṃ sāmudrañ ca tayoḥ parīkṣaṇaṃ | tatra śālyodanapiṇḍam
                        akuthitam avidagdhaṃ | rajatabhājanopahitaṃ varṣati deve kurvvīta
                        sa cet muhūrttasthitas tādṛśa eva bhavati | tad gāṅgam iti
                        avagantavyaṃ | varṇṇānyatāsitthaprakledo vā tatsāmudram iti vidyāt
                        | tan nopādeyaṃ | sāmudram apy āśvayuji māsi gṛhītaṃ gāṅgavad
                        bhavati | tad upādeyam iti | śuklapaṭaikadeśapracyutam athavā
                        harmmyatalaparibhraṣṭam anyair vvā prayogair ggṛhītaṃ śailabhājane
                        śailavan mṛnmaye vā pātreṣv anuguptan nidadhyāt | tat sarvvakālam
                        upayuñjīta | tasyālābhe bhaumaṃ | tat punaḥ saptavidhaṃ | tad
                        yathā kaupan nādeyaṃ sārasan tāḍāga m prāsravaṇam audbhijaṃ
                        cauṇṭyam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.8">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra varṣāvarṣāsvāntarikṣamaudbhijaṃ vā seveta mahāguṇatvā-t |
                        śaradi sarvvam prasannatvāt | hemante sārasan tāḍāgam vā | vasante
                        kaupaṃ cauṇṭyaṃ prāsrāvaṇam vā | grīṣme 'pyevaṃ | prāvṛṣyendram
                        anabhivṛṣṭaṃ sarvvaṃ eva | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.9">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.9</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kīṭamūtrapurīṣāṇḍaśava-kothapradūṣitaṃ | tṛṇaparṇṇodakayutaṃ
                        kaluṣam viṣasaṃyutaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.10">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.10</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         yo 'vagāheta varṣāsu pibed vāpi navañ jalaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa bāhyābhyantarān rogān labhate kṣipram eva tu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.11">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.11</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra yat paṅkaśevālatṛṇahaṭhapadmaprabhṛtibhir avacchannaṃ
                        raviśaśikiraṇānilair vvātijuṣṭāṃ gandharasopasṛṣṭan tad vyāpannam
                        iti vidyāt | sparśarasarūpagandhavīryavipākāḥ | doṣāḥ ṣaṭ kharatā
                        paicchilyam auṣṇyaṃ dantagrāhitā ca sparśadoṣaḥ |
                        paṅkasikatāśaivālavāhulyādvikṛtavarṇṇatā rūpadoṣaḥ | vyaktarasatā
                        rasadoṣaḥ | aniṣṭagandhatā gandhadoṣaḥ | yad upayuktan
                        tṛṣṇāgauravaśūlakaphaprasekān āpādayati sa vīryadoṣaḥ | yad
                        upayuktaṃ cirād vipacyate viṣṭambhayati sa vipākadoṣaḥ || ta ete
                        āntarikṣe doṣā na bhavanti | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.12">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.12</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         vyāpanne cāgnikvathanaṃ sūryātapanam ayam piṇḍataptanirvvāpaṇam
                        vā prasādhakam bhavati</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.13"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.14"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.15"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.16"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.17">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.17</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         saptakaluṣasya prasādhakāni bhvanti | tad yathā ||
                        katakagomedakavisagranthiparṇṇīmūlaśevālavastrāṇimuktāmaṇiś ceti
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.19">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.19</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         saptaśītīkaraṇāni bhavanti | tad yathā || pravātasthāpanam
                        dakaprakṣepanaṃ yaṣṭibhrāmaṇam vyajanaṃ | vastroddharaṇaṃ |
                        vālukāprakṣepaṇaṃ sikyāvalam vanañ ceti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.18">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.18</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pañca nikṣepaṇāni bhavanti | tad yathā | phalakaṃ tryaṣṭakaṃ
                        muñjāvalayaṃ dakamañ cikāśikyakañ ceti | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.12a">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.12a</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nāgapuṣpacampakotpalapāṭalāprabhṛtibhiś cādhivāsanam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.20">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.20</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sugandhavispaṣṭarasaṃ suśītan tarṣanāśanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         acchaṃ laghu ca hṛdyañ ca toyaṅ guṇavad ucyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.21">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.21</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra nadyaḥ paścimābhimukhāḥ pathyā laghūdakatvāt |
                        pūrvvābhimukhā na praśasyante gurūdakatvāt | dakṣiṇābhimukhā
                        nātidoṣalā bhavanti | sādhāraṇatvāt | tatra sahyaprabhavāḥ kuṣṭhañ
                        janayanti | vindhyaprabhavā kuṣṭhaṃ hṛdrogañ ca | malayaprabhavāḥ
                        krimīn | mahendraprabhavāḥ ślīpadodarāṇi | himavatprabhavāḥ |
                        galagaṇḍaṃ kvacid gaṇḍamālāṃ | prācyāvanty āparāvantyāś cārśāṃsy
                        upajanayanti | tatra pāriyātraprabhavā valārogyakarā iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.22">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.22</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         nadyaḥ śīghravahā laghvyaḥ proktā yāś cāmalodakāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         gurvvyaḥ śaivālakaluṣajalaudyāmandagāś ca yāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.23"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.24">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.24</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra sarvveṣāṃ bhaumānām pratyūṣasi grahaṇaṃ | tatra hi
                        śaityalāghavam adhikam bhavati | śaityañ cāparo guṇa iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.25">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.25</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         divārkkakiraṇair jjuṣṭaṃ juṣtam indukarair nniśi |
                        <caesura/>
                         arūkṣam anabhiṣyandi tattulyaṃ gaganāmbunā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.26">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.26</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         gaganāmbu tridoṣaghnaṃ gṛhītaṃ yat subhājane |
                        <caesura/>
                         balyaṃ rasāyanaṃ śītaṃ mātrāpekṣan tataḥ paraṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.27ab">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.27ab</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         raktoghnaṃ śītalaṃ hlādi jvaradāhastṛṣāpahaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.28">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.28</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         mūrcchāpittoṣmadāheṣu viṣe rakte mādatyaye ||
                        <caesura/>
                         bhramaklamaparīteṣu tamake vamathau tathā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.29">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.29</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ūrddhage raktapitte ca śītamambhaḥ praśasyate ||
                        <caesura/>
                         pārśvaśūlapratiśyāye vātaroge galagrahe | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.30">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.30</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ādhmāte stimite kāṣṭhe sadyaḥśuddhe navajvare ||
                        <caesura/>
                         hikkāyāṃ snehapīte ca śītāmbu parivarjjayet | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.49">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.49</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         gavyan tu śitasnigdhamadhuram avidāhi
                        vātapittaśleṣmaśoṇitamānaseṣu vikāreṣv aviruddhaṃ |
                        jīrṇṇajvarakāsaśophakṣayaraktapittagulmodaramūrcchābhramamadapipāsāpāṇḍurogārśa
                        udāvarttātīsārayonirogagarbhbhāsrāvaśramaklamaharam valyaṃ vṛṣyaṃ
                        rasāyanaṃ medhyaṃ vyājīkakaraṇaṃ sandhānam āsthāpanam āyuṣyam
                        vamanam virecanañ ceti || thāpanaṃ tulyaguṇatvāc caujaso vardhanaṃ
                        bālavṛddhakṣatakṣīṇānāṃ kṣudvyavāyavyāyāmakarśitānāṃ ca
                        pathyatamam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.50"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.51"/>

                        <caesura/>
                         ajānām alpakāyatvāt kaṭutiktaniṣevaṇāt | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.53">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.53</label>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.54">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.54</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śophagulmodarārśoghnaṃ krimikuṣṭhakaphāpahaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         āvikaṃ madhuraṃ snigdhaṃ guru pittakaphapahaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.55">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.55</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         pathyaṃ kevalavāteṣu kāse cānilasambhave ||
                        <caesura/>
                         mahābhiṣyandi madhuraṃ māhiṣam vahniśādanaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.56">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.56</label>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.57">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.45.57</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         madhurāmlagsaṃ rūkṣaṃ lavaṇānurasaṃ laghu ||
                        <caesura/>
                         nāryās tu madhruaṃ stanyaṅ kaṣāyānurasaṃ himaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.58">

                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 46, draft based on MS H]</head>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.1">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.1</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         athāto 'nnapānavidhim vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.3">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.3</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dhanvantarim abhivādya suśruta uvāca ||
                        <caesura/>
                         bhagavan prāgabhihitam prāṇināṃ mūlam āhāro balavarṇṇaujasāñ ca
                        saḥ ṣaṭsu raseṣv āyatto rasāḥ punar dravyāśrayiṇaḥ |
                        dravyarasavīryavipākanimitte ca kṣayavṛddhī doṣāṇāṃ sātmyañ ca |
                        brahmāder api ca lokasyāhāraḥ sthityutpattihetur
                        āhārādevābhivṛddhir balam ārogyavarṇendriyaprasādaś ca | tathā hy
                        āhāravaiṣampādasvāsthyan tasyāsitapītalīḍhakhāditasya
                        nānādravyātmakasyānekavidhavikalpaprabhāvasya pṛthak pṛthak
                        dravyarasavīryavipākakarmmecchāṃ jñātuṃ na hy
                        anavabuddhadravyasvabhāvā bhiṣajo roganigrahaṅ karttuṃ samarthā
                        ity āhārāyattāś ca prāṇino yasmāt tasmād annapānavidhim upadiśat
                        tu me bhagavān ity uktaḥ provāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ
                        <caesura/>
                         || atha khalu vatsa suśruta || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.4">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.4</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra
                        lohitakaśālikalamakakarddamakapāṇḍukasugandhakasakunāhṛtakuṣmāṇḍakapuṇḍarīkamahāśāliśītabhīrukalodhraśūkadīrghaśūkakāñcanakahāyanakadūṣīmahākhyaprabhṛtayaḥ
                        śālayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.5">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.5</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         madhurā vīryataḥ śītā vipākā kaṭukāḥ smṛtāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pittaghnālpānilakaphaḥ snigdhā vaddhālpavarccasaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.6">

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.7">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.7</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmād alpāntaraguṇāḥ kramaśaḥ śālayo pare || </l>

                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.8</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ṣaṣṭikakāṅgakamukundakapītakapramodakakālakāsanapuṣpakamahāsvetakamahāvrīhicūrṇṇakakuravakedāraprabhṛtayo
                        vrīhayaḥ || </l>

                        <caesura/>
                         śālīnāṅguṇataś cāpi samānā vaddhavarccasaḥ || </l>

                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.10</label>

                        <caesura/>

                            n="2"/>tayo vrīhayaḥ || </l>

                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.37</label>

                        <caesura/>

                    <!-- start of the lavaṇa varga, 313-330 -->
                    <!-- <lg type="varga"> -->
                    <p ana="subheading" style="bold">[<hi>Lavaṇavarga</hi>]</p>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.313">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.313</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         saindhavasāmudraviḍasauvarccalaromakodbhidaprabhṛtīni yathottaram
                        uṣṇāni vātaharāṇi kaphapittakarāṇi || kaṭupākīni yathāpūrvvaṃ
                        snigdhāni svādūni sṛṣṭamūtrapurīṣāṇi ceti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.314">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.314</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         cakṣuṣyaṃ saindhavaṃ hṛdyaṃ rucyaṃlaghvagnidīpanaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         snigdham vṛṣyaṃ samadhuraṃ śītan doṣaghnam uttamaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.315">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.315</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sāmudraṃ madhuram pāke nātyuṣṇam avidāhi ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhedanaṃ snigdhamīṣac ca śītaghnan nātipittalaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.316">

                         sāmlaṃ satīkṣṇaṃ sahimaṃ pānakaṃ syān niratyayaṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.432">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.432</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         tatra pūrvvaśasya jā tānām vedarāmlaṃ | vaidalānān dhāmlaṃ |
                        jāṅgalānān mṛgānān dhanvajānām pakṣiṇāñ ca pippalyāsavaḥ |
                        viṣkirāṇāṃ kolavadarāsavaḥ | pratudānāṃ kṣīravṛksāsavaḥ | guhe
                        śayānāṃ kharjjūranālikerāsavaḥ | sāmudrāṇām mātuluṅgāsavaḥ |
                        kus̤māṇḍānām amlānām sārdvīkāsavaḥ | amlā amlānāṃ phalānāṃ
                        padmotpalakandāsavaḥ | kaṣāyāṇāṃ dāḍimavetrāsavaḥ | madhurāṇāṃ
                        trikaṭukayuktaḥ khadirāsavaḥ | tālaphalādīnāṃ dhānyāmlaṃ |
                        kandānāṃ dūrvvānalavetrāsavaḥ | pippalyādīnāṃ
                        svadaṃṣṭrāvasukāsavaḥ | cuccūprabhṛtīnāṃ lodhrāsavaḥ |
                        kusumbhaśākasya tad eva | maṇḍūkaparṇyādīnām mahāpañcamūlyāsavaḥ |
                        tālamastakādīnām amlaphalāsavaḥ | saindhavādīnāṃ surāsavam
                        āranālan toyam vā || </l>

                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.512">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.512</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         svalpaṃ yadā doṣavivandhamāmaṃ
                        <caesura/>
                         līnan na tejaḥ patham āvṛṇoti |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavanty ajīrṇṇe 'pi tadā bubhukṣā
                        <caesura/>
                         sā mandavṛddhim viṣavan nihanti ||</l>
                    <!-- </lg> -->
                    <!-- <lg type="varga"> -->
                    <p ana="subheading" style="bold">[<hi>The twenty guṇas and their
                            actions</hi>]</p>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.513">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.513</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ata ūrddhvam pravakṣyāmi guṇānāṅ karmmavistaraṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         karmmabhis tv anumīyante nānā dravyāśrayā guṇāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.518cd">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.518cd</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         daśādyāḥ karmmataḥ proktās teṣāṅ karmmaviśeṣaṇaiḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.519ab">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.519ab</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         daśaivādyām pravakṣyāmi dravādīs tāṃś chṛṇuśva me ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.514">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.514</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         śītaḥ prahlādanastambhī mūrcchātṛṭsvedadāhajit ||1||
                        <caesura/>
                         uṣṇas tad viparītaḥ syāt pācanaś ca viśeṣataḥ ||2||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.515">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.515</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sneho mārddavakṛt snigdho balavarṇṇakaras tathā ||3||
                        <caesura/>
                         rūkṣas tad viparītaḥ syād viśeṣāt stambhanaḥ smṛtaḥ ||4||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.516">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.516</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         picchilo jīvanaśleṣī sandhāno vṛṃhaṇas tathā ||5||
                        <caesura/>
                         viṣado viparīto 'sya bhedī śodhanaropaṇaḥ ||6||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.517">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.517</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dāhapākakaras tīkṣṇaḥ śrāvaṇo mṛdur anyathā ||8||
                        <caesura/>
                         sāndropalepaḥ kaphakṛd guruḥ prīṇanabṛṃhaṇaḥ ||10||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.518ab">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.518ab</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         laghus tad viparītaḥ syāl lekhano ropaṇas tathā ||11||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.519cd">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.519cd</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dravaḥ prakledanaḥ sāndraḥ śuṣkaḥ syād dvandvakārakaḥ ||13||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.519ef">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.519ef</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ślakṣṇaḥ picchilavaj jñeyaḥ karkkaśo viṣado yathā ||15||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.520">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.520</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sukhānuvarttī sūkṣmañ ca sugandhīrocano mataḥ ||16||
                        <caesura/>
                         durggandho viparīto sya prakāśau cāpy ubhāv api ||17||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.521">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.521</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         saro 'nulomanaḥ prokto mando yātrākaraḥ smṛtaḥ ||19||
                        <caesura/>
                         vyavāyī deham akhilaṃ vyāpya pākāya kalpate ||20||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.522"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.523">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.523</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         guṇā viṃśatir ity ete karmmataḥ parikīrttitāḥ ||</l>
                    <!-- </lg> -->
                    <!-- <lg type="varga"> -->
                    <p ana="subheading" style="bold">[<hi>Metabolic process</hi>]</p>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.524">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.524</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         ata ūrddham pravakṣyāmi āhāragatiniścayaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pañcabhūtātmake dehe āhāraḥ pākabhautikaḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         vipakvaḥ pañcadhā samyag guṇāṃs tān abhivarddhayet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.525">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.525</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         avidagdhaṃ kaphaṃ pittam vidagdhaḥ pavanam punaḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         samyag vipakṣo niḥsāra āhāraḥ parivṛṃhayet |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.526">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.526</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         viṇmūtram āhāramalaḥ sāraḥ prāgīrito rasaḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         sa tu vyānena vikṣiptaḥ sarvvān dhātūn visarppati |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.527">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.527</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphapittamalaḥ kheṣu svedaḥ syān nakharoma ca ||
                        <caesura/>
                         netraviṭ tvakṣu ca sneho dhātūnāṃ kramaśo malāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.528">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.528</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         divāvivuddhahṛdaye jāgrataḥ puṇḍarīkavat ||
                        <caesura/>
                         anupaklinna dhātvannam ajīrṇṇe 'pi hitaṃ niśi |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.529">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.529</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         hṛdayaṃ līyate rātrau prasuptasya viśeṣataḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         samupaklinnadhātvannam ajīrṇṇe tvahitaṃ divā ||</l>
                    <!-- </lg> -->

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.530">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.530</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         imam vidhiṃ yo 'numatam mahāmuner
                        <caesura/>
                         mmaharṣimukhyasya paṭhet tu yatnataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa bhūmipālo ya vidhātum auṣadham
                        <caesura/>
                         mahātmanāñ cārhati vaidyasattama iti || o ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.531">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.531</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         dravyajñānaṃ rasajñānam vasanañ ca virecanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dravadravyaparijñānam annapānena ṣaṭ smṛtaḥ || o ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.532">
                        <label xml:lang="en">1931 ed. 1.46.532</label>
                        <caesura/>
                         sūtrasthāne purā proktañ catvāriṃśat ṣaḍuttaraṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         adhyāyāḥ kāśirājena pūrṇṇaṃ sarvvaṃ savistaraṃ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.trailer">|| iti suśrute śalyatantre sūtrasthānaṃ
                        samāptaṃ || ||</l>
